soo moche ye shall well perceiue thinges harte sore desyreth bringe passe egally good euyll bothe oftentimes selfe thinking misery many yeres haue benne wrapped semeth shall styll onlesse moste prudente wysedomes woll prouide remedy wonte call remembraunce wretched life shal leade time come without set selfe libertie nede reherse selfe beare well inoughe remembraunce howe many dyuers hurtes griefes haue endured sithe moste common wele crueltie certayne vngratious persones permitted let slippe vnder rule order power fewe suche began take vpon rest besyde lettinge passe reherse mishappe chaunce ech v hath maye one regarde beholde v noble stronge valiante men whiche often tymes common weale haue eschewed perylles moste greate greuous hauynge neyther lande rent lefte wretch nedy sorowfull caste haue moche defende liues fame citie goodes whiche violate vexe trouble together bothe lawe god onely walowinge rich welthe pleasantlye passe awaye theyr tyme luste also euery thynge beinge done theyr commaundement wyl seke wayes meanes attrappe destroye moste noble valiant men citie selfe doubte nothinge finallye theye haue exercise regall power haue word greuous name royal power surely theyr power greatter kinges kingdome euer mo kynges one tyme kinge euer mightie soo stronge whiche power constitute make kynges men haue full power rule prouinces depriue free nacions theyr landes geue dispose mennes royalmes kyngedomes men whole world kynges prince straunge nacions haue ben alwaies tributours haue power fauoure ryches worshyp honoure satisfiynge whole couetousenes surelye semeth whole worlde lyttell ouer straite nowe wolde seeke haue power rich honoure shulde v greuous yet mought suffered borne endure suffer hauynge abundance cattell golde syluer iuorie ryche lyfe sore thretened perpetuall peryll dreede oure iudgementes puttynge roumes office prepared whyche thynges howe longe wyll valiaunte noble men pacientlye beare suffer better man thousande tymes dye lyue citye abiecte contemned despised desperate forsaken tremblynge quakynge mistrustinge owne affaire hardye speke without lybertie without auctorite wythout shappe free man yea subiecte whiche wee common weale wolde feare dreede v wherfore moste hardy valiant men let v laste shake stuggishenesse let v take suche hart courage besemeth noble romaynes borne forefather coulde suffre proude kynge tarquimus canne suffer one kynge many moste cruell tyrantes surely neuer leaue wyll monishe wyll teache instructe wyll alwaye declare thynke beste done shall tyme escape neyther night daye woll minde imagine soo euer concerninge oure libertye ought thought thynge oughte entreprised done wyll make courtsye doo shall desyre praye haue doinge therof fynally wyll becometh worthy romayne libertie wyll put life ieoperdy protest god man victorie handes wyll playe men haue hande syllas souldiours withe theyr fauour strengthe one assente redye ayde v whose sodeyne commynge shall shortelye haue stronge sure hoste men like diligence fauour loue recouer libertie moste bolde valiante men gn piso p siccinius nucerius haue conspired v whiche tone hither spayne great armye tother capytayne ruleth mauritaine two shal haue felowes counsaylynge moste trusty sure helper nedes busynesse menne good lorde route withe fauoure hardy courage agree v recouer liberte let passe speake noble citizen whiche hauinge neither lande rent left wrapped great wretchednesse nede vnneth suffer endure noble mighty citie shoulde subiecte wyll power fewe person moste noble valiante men whose ryches worshyp honour prouynces roumes offyces hyghe auctorities dere pleasante whereto shulde reherse good wylles poore men whiche vnfortunate felowes beinge oppressed excedynge greate dette trouble infinite wronges safe sure none meane ciuile warre nedethe remembre men whiche nede whiche priuate iniuries whiche feare iugementes necessitie compellethe vnto warre swere faythe citizen without dominacion mighty men whiche wold al harte resiste withstande cruell tyrantes ouer many redy recouer liberti market place ful men al townes italye ful italie reysed vp men al state condicion finally men euery age agree consent one thynge doth litle helpe forwarde rich men spited amonge stronge nation theyr might hated consul power withe whiche next election truste shal se adourned doubte beinge consul capitaine souldioures myndes styrred kendeled herto italy conspiring v recouer agayne libertie goddes sake moste strong valiant men let slyppe take sure holde occasion offered vnto last cal remembraunce romaine prince haue suche time neuer man hadde v lette scape shall neuer haue suche tyme agayne longe exhortinge nothynge elles monishe man foolyshe perceiueth none way saftie wherfore necessitie perill large rewardes shal aryse thys warre shoulde moche stere prouoke therto mine ooracion shal haue bee capitaine elles companion rather bothe twayne neyther mynde body shal euer fayle although mynde corage hath euer ben prompte redy yet time hathe fayled v alwaye soone oportunite appered selfe chiefe principal wold haue recouered agayne libertie soo beinge consull prince auctoures capitaines goddes afraied thy mischeuous dedes thine oracion time thy mocions coniected willingly againste made afraied feare great assemblye senatours greate companye noble cityzens could trouble innocent mynd accusacion thing dyd thy oracion meane shuld flee thou saieste deedes well knowen mine imaginacios clerer lyght doest thou nowe perswade flee hauinge power defence myne owne aboute senate presente whyche wyll prohibite let harme shewe forth mischeuous dedes open plainely sedicion punyshemente besemeth mercifull great peril delay without helpe maye hurtful thou haue principall conspiracie waxe colde thou seeste myschaunce thou preparest either common weale shall lyghte vppon thy selfe thys thynge nowe thy greate daunger farre otherwyse handled thou thoughtest doubtest nowe woll obiecte againste thy goodes dyddest thou thynke wolde come senate therefore came thou forthwith sore afraied thynkest thou nowe make afraied wyth thy threatninges knoweste thou howe free howe bolde stomake innocente wylte thou cicero flee surelye wyll flee abyde ouercome thy proude bragges muste nedes reproue thy mischeuous deedes inuencions let thy witness come place thou saiest thou hast great plentie cesar delyuered certayne letter louyngly wrytten vndiscrete man beare vnto hym whiche whan came cesars house informed porter cesar senate streyghte waye rude felowe came senate delyuered letter cesar senate called hym drunkarde naturally verye sobre propertye loue suche delectation oftentymes cause man noble fyle hym selfe blotte fylthynes shame pl vectius accuseth c cesar culpable conspiracye cesar clereth reuengeth hym selfe cap xliiii bvt sone happened thynge troubled cesars mynde l vectius accused hym noui questor culpable conspiracy q curius broughte hym greate hatred bycause named hym senate parte taker conspiratours vectius promysed brynge forth catilyns owne handewritynge curius sayde knewe catilyne cesar takyng greuousely shulde spotted wyth soo shamefull blotte came senate purge hym selfe senate syttyng longer accustomed excedynge multitude common people ranne thyther greate haste troublous people demed senate wolde decre greuous thyng agaynst cesar inflamed wyth loue sturred peryll beganne make greate shout seditiousely required senate let cesar go cato withdrawe cesar occasion sedition perswaded senate diuyde amonge comon people rome greate quantitie wheate whiche liberalitie hartis poore cominaltie meruelously reconciled cato senate comons hate nigardes fauoure plentyfull liberall loue largesse ledde wyth great feastes moued play bowed gyftes giftes men myndes blynded pafter cesar made oration whiche oration declared none conspiratours also opened consull certaine thinges cosperacy wha lamentablye red cicero wytnesse cicero clered hym suspition thus dyd consull either bicause knew nothing certainly charge cesar el bicause thought best wynke matter though cesar crassus myght haue bene manifestly conuicted yet coulde haue bene punyshed seynge tone theim surely fenced wyth excedynge greatte rychesse tother fauour people pbut afterwarde cesar vehemently inuehed ageinste l vectius whan hadde oration torne hym sharpe wordes spoylinge hym householde stouffe taking pledge surety greuousely punyshed hym caste nouius questor prison bycause suffred pretor aboue hym auttoritie plede hym higher offycers maye commaunded theyr inferiours equalles ceaser beinge content herewyth broughte passe curius shoulde gyuen rewardes whiche vnto hym bycause fyrste detected conspyracye decreed mooste ample wyse retourne agayne lefte whan nede ully speake caesar execucion lentulus felowes cap xlv fifte daye december drewe towarde euenynge longe consultacion senate lengthe decreed aforesaide accordinge catos sentence execucion shoulde doone founde gyltie wherfore consul thought best preuent night hande leste meane space myschefull cursed parte myght plaide thoughte force violence deliuer set large oute senate house came accompanied senatoures knyghtes rome yonge men noble bloudde armed thence wente house hadde custodye caste fyrste brought lentulus keepynge lentulus spynther palayce waye callyd sacrum uia throughe myddes markette place vnto prysone wayes vytayles shulde come opteine vyctorye without stroke strikinge shuld abide tyll two hostis inclosed betwene also feared leste longe delayeng army wolde slyppe many fledde frome whan tydinges lentulus hath brought hym selfe v nowe taryeng succour come frome citie nowe passe fraunce nowe perceyue well case stande oure ennemyes haue two hostes tone wyll suffre v drawe citie tother doth let v lybertie oure lyues nede fyght fewe maye myghty strog wherfore set vpon boldly remembrynge noble actes ye haue done tyme past ye myghte haue ledde forth lyues exile greate shame reproche hauynge none youre selues myght haue gaped longe inough rome vppon goodes ryches bycause facion semed vnto beinge men shamefull intollerable ye determyne take waye ye wyll relynquishe thynges behoueth bolde man excepte conquerour changeth warre peace hope saue selfe flyghte whan ye returne backes throwe awaye armour wherewith youre bodyes defended verye madnesse euermore batayle greatest peryll mooste fearefull boldenesse stede stronge wall whan consyder youe souldyours whan ponder youre dedes greatte hope vyctory enbraceth youre lustye stomackes youre youthe strengthe encourageth farther oure good great oportunitie goddis immortall sayde sygnifye v vyctorye lyke wee alwayes desyred souldiours alredye encouraged fyght hereafter shall haue suche occasyon catilyne maye gette fraunce shall vnderstandeth yf catiline shulde tyme whiche god forbyde ouer come v shulde endure onelye cruell proude domination also infamous full myschiefe shulde dare refuse maner sharpe punyshement youe knowe catilyns crueltie youe knowe nothinge hym braynsyke boldnes pryde sensualitie viciousnesse selfe wyll knowe hys frendes ye knowe kynrede vnyuersally dycers drunkardes murderer theyr parentes moste mischefull promysed gyue citie theues spoyle nowe appoynte dyuide amonge selfes goodes manours house onelye desyre goodes also beynge angrie couet oure bloudde pastyme moore pleasant effusion bloudde hangynge beatinge see citesyns tourmented theyr face theyr solace wer wonte drynke mennes bloudde whose bloudde trowe ye nowe soo greatte thryste hatred good menne wolle spare spyll therfore wyll horseman whiche though se horse gallop lustily yet voyce spurres courage likewise exhort kendled thynges vehemently starred defende lybertie sayde pricke forwardes rounne redye wherfore beseche forefather theyr many folde labour vyctories manye yeres space conquered got ye shal nowe fight glorye trybutes reuenge iniuryes done frendes whyche romanye armye alwaye wonte entre battayle common weale temple goddes immortall goodes aultars oratory lyues wyues chyldern libertie fynallye healthe worlde muste contende horrible cruel beast whych fallen dyche lette hym ouerwhelmed behynde afore weale dydde euer lamentablye desyre prowesse helpe fortitude souldiours tyme saye requyreth whyche beinge fyre weapon wycked conspy ye sheweth selfe maner speaketh thus p haue endured many thynges citie freedome suffered tyme day night hath ben caytiues haue wrought myscheuous dyspleasure murther hath ben doone many yeres without theym vngratious abhomynable dede without though thynges aforesayde intollerable yet coulde bare theym nowe endure togither one man sake shoulde stande drede mooste greattest daunger wherfore moste valiaunt souldiours beseche praye suffre deliuered diuine counsel consul prudence snare deceytes lentulus inward enemy oppressed cursed theft man moreouer comende vnto castel capitoll walles citie auters sepulcres forefather lawes customes libertie forfathers contended battayle onely bondage also rule comande ought escape horryble moste cruell dominion vncleane thefe wherefore moste valyaunt souldyours seynge matter brought great ieoperdy eyther ye must day reteyne styll feate armes propper lybertie romaynes name elles ye must preferre deathe aboue bondage yuell doer whiche victoriousely ye shall vanquyshe shall also theyr parentes sleing punyshed helle yf happe slayn battayle ye shall opteyne come place good blessyd menne word countrey speaketh vnto nowe harken vnto p seynge good souldyours many dyuerse kyndes deathe hange ouer men semeth ought rather reioyce sorye yf sorte dethe whiche mooste goodly dye oure countreye shoulde chaunce vnto v deathe libertie cytie myght reteyned stylle lyfe shorte course glorye eternall seynge euery manne muste dye shoulde desyre mooste specyally dye countrey though lyue bodylye yet shall lyue perpetuall glorye nowe trewely shulde repelled deathe maye eschewe withoute shedynge bloudde whiche thynge ye maye better vnderstande wylle declare sortes people noble army catilins gatheryd togyther saye conflate gathered togyther three kyndes men fyrste kynde sylla sente inhabyte towne fesules menne bycause haue wasted awaye theyr owne goodes looke catylyne shoulde gyue theym newe table prescription ryche menne haue forgotte howe sodeynely syllas tyme poore menne made ryche actes iugurth trewe whiche longe harde report comen fame tha noble iugurth fauoure bothe dedes commendacion scipio moued mynde chaunged fro forsayd purpose forther intended oppresse iugurthe malyce enuy concluded attempt ouercome benefites kindnesse thentent ouercome shulde tyme come fynde hert pyte indommage hym heyres sone purpose micipsa adopted iugurth vnto sonne farthermore decreed ordayned testament iugurth shulde one heyres partener possession kingdome togyder two natural sone adherbal hiempsall fewe yeres ordinaunce micipsa age sykenesse drew nere vnto end lyfe consumed age disease wherfore consideryng deth fast approchynge sayd called iugurth many frendes kynsmen also presece two natural sone adherbal hiempsal iugurth wordes herafter insue folowe pthe exortacion kyng micipsa lytell deth iugurth vi chapter mi dere sonne iugurth knowe oute remembrauce howe ye lost father brother charitably louingly receiued yonge tender age kyngdome tyme ye warre without rich wythout conforte without hope comferte ryches lykely haue bene cast awaye dyd thinkyng benefytes kyndnesse shoulde bee vnto lesse intyerly beloued myne owne naturall chyldren body begotten certainly thing hath disceiued ouerpasse great magnificente excellente dedes valyauntly done specially last comynge warre numace ye greatly adourned inhaunced honoure glory bothe mine owne person kingdome romaynes fore time frendes vnto v vertue manlye actes ye haue establyshed amitie frendes made moche moore frendes hispayne name glorie oure householde manhode renouate renewed thus finally ye haue ouercome enuie yl willers onely glorious actes valiaunt interprises whiche one moost difficultie wherfore nowe sonne iugurth sithe nature hath nere concluded ende life admonishe charge exhorte faith right hand faith fidelite ye owe kingdome obtest require ye loue meintaine cherishe two sonnes adherbal hiempsall whiche kinnered nere benefite kindnes bretherene vnto forthremore exhorte ye counte better moore pleasure acquainte conioine vnto youe forayns straungers rather ret yne suche ioyned natural blode kynred neyther great army men habundance treasours ye chefe socours defence kyngdome oche rather trusty faythfull frendes whome man canne neyther compelled force armes yet bye golde syluer parseuer stedfast amyte optayned kept kyndnesse good dedes fidelite faythfulnes among frendes frendlye stedfaste amyte brother brother certaynly none ought louyng natural inclination strauger shal ye fynd faythful trusty ye shewe selfe ennemy owne kynsmen forsothe ye contynue togyder honest good louyng agreable concorde bytwene selfe thanne kyngdome committe gaue vnto shall continue sure stedfast nowe cotrarely ye yll disagreynge among selfe ye shal short season make ryght poore feble incertayne loue peace concorde small ryches small lordshyppes generally al smal thynges increase multiplie discorde grettest thynges worlde decay fall vtterly ruyne sonne iugurthe cause ye passe myne two naturall sonnes age wysdome therfore semeth moche make suche wyse prouision bothe selfe also nothyng happen wyse well euery stryffe debate howe whiche mightyer rycher often suffreth iniury neuerthelesse semeth dothe wronge thanne feble aduersary ye dere sonnes adherball hiempsall se ye worshipe loue iugurth worthy vncle bewar ye nat offende dysplease hym folow vertue manly behauour deuoir best power example behauynge selfe discretly wysely nat hereafter reported haue taken vnto adoption better chyldren haue begotte thus concluded kyng micipsa word howe iugurth well perceyued kynges wordes fayned spoken agaynst herte remedy myghte haue bene founde neuertheles answered benygnely tyme thought reuoulued mynde moche otherwyse contrary humble mylde answere phowe kyng mycipsa departed lyfe fyrst cause dissencion discord betwene iugurth herball hiempsall vii chapter long kynge micipsa decessed whose deathe dolourous sore bewayled subiectes naturall sonnes lamented without greate cause processe hystorie shall afterwarde declare kynges funerall exequies magnificentlye ended appertayned state royal thre prince say adherball hiempsall iugurth anone assembled intent commen treate busyness royalme concernynge particion separation thinges conuenient whan shuld sytte take theyr place order hiempsal yongest thre somewhat fiers nature disposed statelynesse mynd longe time disdained ignobilitie iugurth asmoche vnlike vnto birth towchinge mother side bastard borne said wherefore disdained iugurthe shulde haue place moost honoure amonge whiche naturall sonnes kinge also laufully borne contempte iugurth set selfe downe ryght hande brother adherball thintent iugurth shulde syt myddes bytwene whiche rowme numidiens count honour afterwarde howe brother adherball requyred ofte giue place iugurth bycause age yet vnnethes coude moche paine induce hym therto last fatygate requestes brother noble men realme chaunged place set hym vpon side countenance declarynge mynde contented thus last satte iugurth age middes bitwene bothe place moost honoure whan thre prynces thus sette communed many thinges concernynge administracion kyngdome amonge many dyuers thinges iugurth sayde statute ordinaunces kynge micipsa made fyue yeres deth ought congruence adnulled none effecte season sayde hys witte age syckenesse feble dull small valoure therfore suche thinges space enacted done without wisdome reason whan hiempsall herde iugurth thus speke answered sayenge pleased right well shuld done within thre yeres said father micipsa hath adopted sonne testament ordained partiner kigdome whiche worst vnaduised dede euer dyd yonge olde wherfore iugurthe according youre owne ordinaunce must fyrst af al adnulled broken whiche done brother shall greatly contende remenaunt wordes hiempsal pearsed hart iugurth profou dely man thoughte suspected wherfore frome tyme forwarde wrathe wordes drede losse porcyon kyngdome mynde great trouble anguyshe somoche then forthe went aboute ymagyned ordained onely reuoulued mind gile treaso hiempsal might caught daunger whan purpose proceded slowly forwarde considerynge frowarde desire vnresonable appetite mynde coud mytigated pacified cocluded bring enterprise effect maner meanes preuye treason gyle el euydent open violence force armes retourne agayne lefte thys first assemble thre prince whiche spake pleased treasours kinge micipsa shulde deuided among bicause dissencion also march boundes eche theyr dominion seuerally shulde assigned eche hys porcion wherfore tyme appoynted prefixed whanne bothe shulde doone tyme departe treasoures sooner assigned deuyde limitte boundes theyre dominion appointement made prince departed company mynde iugurth lytell inquieted sayde checke hiempsall whiche cause awayted tyme reuenge hym phowe iugurth reason murdred hiempsall yonger sonne ynge micipsa viii chapter whan thre prynces departed der haue sayd soiourned sondrye place nere towre treasure laye hiempsall drewe towne named thirmida far distant whiche towne dwellyng place tha happened towne man gard longing iugurth lorde ryght derele beloued greatly fauour seruaunt iugurth moche conuersaunte familyer ye house house hiempsall often done tyme bi meanes craft counterfayte kayes gate brynge vnto hym right kayes gate locked nyghtly delyuered vnto hiempsall hym selfe soo myght nat vnmyssed space nyght whan iugurth induced numidian consent dede promysed hym self win short time come sayd lodgyng hiempsal tyme ye case shuld requyre great power armed men numydyan shorte tyme perfourmed commaundemente iugurth somoche brought vnto hym counterfayted key apoynted iugurth gladde mynde anone prepared secretly great company armed men whome commaunded bringe vnto heed hiempsal trenched body executynge dede commaunded al ruled numidyan counterfayted key done sayd numidian connayed armed men preuyly nyght house hiempsall lyke infourmed iugurth whan tratoure satellyte entred company broken warde edifice diuers serched prince hiempsal som murdred seruauntes lay slepenge theyr beddys suspectynge suche treason wakened dynne stert vp mette theyr enemyes defendynge selfe al vayne leyser arme selfe therfore slayne anone vnarmed men armed apointed myschefe whan treatours longe sought hiempsall myght nat fynde hym serched nerely euery hyd corner secret close place braste open full dynne mengled noyse clamour moche sought nerely last founde hiempsal hyd cotage poore seruynge woman whiche place fled begynnyg affraye man astonyed drede ignorant place anone numidian foude slewe without mecri commaunded cutte hed brought iugurth shortly ye fame cruell tyrannous dede diuulgate ouer spred landes affrike adherball whiche vnder subieccion micipsa whyle lyued sore troubled abasshed fere tyrannous crueltie iugurth numidian anone duyded themselfe two party moost part drewe leaned adherball suche manly best batayle drew parte leaned iugurth wherfore made redy great armie myght ioininge vnto bringing vnder subieccion townes city numidi violence theyr owne volutary insomoch finally kept vnder subieccion bondage hole lande numidy notwithstanding adherbal sent embassadours rome certify senatours ye deth brother cowardly murdred also informe miserable fortune case neuer thelesse made himselfe redy fyght iugurth trust confidence multitude souldyours assembled redy batayle phowe nowe iugurth assembled hys hoost redy vnto batayle lyke multitude company adharbal sayd moche bolder better experte exercised warre partie adherball people redy apointed armyes approched togider whan worthye chosen father sythe come myserye necessytye constrayneth desyre youre ayde succoures wolde moche rather myghte call youre helpe myne owne merytes agaynste doone merytes forefather suche meanes myne owne deseruynge youre benefytes socours due vnto whiche wolde god neded yf youre socoures myghte soo desyred merytes deseruynge shulde call boldlye vse youre socours duetye myne auncestrye haue doone tymes passed nowe sythe soo honeste lyfe innocencye thys worlde fyndeth lytell surenesse theim selfe wythoute protection moreouer syth power mitigate withstande tyrannous iniurye iugurthe therfore chosen father nowe flede vnto chefe refuge coarted necessitie requyre youre socours constrayned put besynes charge haue done anye pleasure profete vnto whiche thynge greued moost one gretest myseryes ryght worthy senatours kynges haue ben receiued frindshyp fauoure ye haue ouerco battayle el perceyuinge selfe danger doubtefull chaunces fortune haue coueited desyred feloweshype fauour rather theyr owne wele moch co contrarely forefather rote linage massinissa confederated hymselfe people rome secod bataile carthage tyme faythfulnes trusted theyr good wil welth rich optained romains beinge tyme assayled warre euery side theyr rich treasours consumed often batayles thus euident auncestry confederat themself felowship owne defence hope dominion priuate profet onelye fauour loue whiche vnto empire wherfore noble senatours suffre progeny braunches stocke distroied suffer neuew trusty fred massinissa aske helpe socoure vaine prudent father none cause demaud socours saue onely helpe socours men none mater whereof co plaine saue miserable fortune onely neuertheles longeth conueniente magesty people roome prohibite withstande iniurye nat suffer kyngedome dominion anye man sothely linage hath done asmouche desyres euer hath ben redy batails nedes assyst wherfore ye folow precept gratitude ye bere remembraunce merites myne auncestry right honesty yt myne extreme necessite ye ayde socoure restore againe quietnesse whyle ye haue none othere businesse hande whiche maye youe inpedimente enterprise moost discrete father brefely clerly declare vnto complaint myseries also certifie youre excellence moore playnlye myne vnnaturall vnkynde kynseman jugurth cruelte vnknowen vnto youre maiestie father micipsa departing lefte behynde v two brethern naturall lauful sonnes supposynge benefites merites iugurth shulde ioyned wyth v thyrde brother ala muche contrary one v murdred cruell iugurthe blynded insaciable ambicion desyre dominion selfe second brother scarselye wyth greate difficulte haue escaped cruell vnmercifull handes maye doo whether shall rathest flee conforte vnhappye exulate thus desolate infortunate socours comforte stocke kinred extincte dethe grandfather massinissa father micipsa necessite hathe constrayned haue payed generall tribute nature delyuered frome mundayne vexacions naturall deth nere kynsman iugurth moch otherwyse tha came doo hathe cursedlye berefte brother lyfe tyranny myscheuous couetise dominion mine kinsman consanguinite affinite mine frendes cruelte bene also oppressed put dethe one meanes taken captiue put hiepsal dere hart al creature nowe thy life berefte yt thy flourig youth log thy natural hour deth yt cruelte semed al haue done neuertheles thiketh mind chauce thy deth ioyed tha sorowed yu hast onely lost thy life thy kingdom also yu hast escaped chasig flight exile ned pouerty wt al wretchedness misery oppresseth wtout confort socours vnhappy miserable exulate thus throwe downe fro father mariages lytle litle migled ye getulias bicause thei proued oftetimes ye comoditie groud fildes often comutacios changings one wt last thei named selfe numidia say herdme diuided preset day ye cotages tylmens house made long wt croked side couerturs bowing iward thei wer belies ship trasuersed turned vp set downe touching ye medea armeniens thei ioyned self wt libies ye medeans armeniens dwelled inward part affrike ye parte possession numidian much dyd yt al nacions subdued wer called numidian ye name ouercomers haue declared ye getulians libies wer first inhabitates affrike perseans medea feare treason noble hertes great courage drew theyr harnes resysted theyr enemy valyantly fully assured prefyxed dye lyke men yf fortune shuld graunt none meanes escape instant danger cowardes hydde theim selfe caues secrete place yf might fynde boldest vsed suche chaunces conforted theyr felowes whiche ferefull vnexpert chaunces warre beit none al bolde well assured hymselfe bothe great drede daunger maruayle euery place sydes inuironed compasse great violence plenteous noumber theyr ennemyes hidde vnder darkenesse nyghte cloudes vtterly obscured starres lyghte theyr peryll indifferente aray set agayne order iiii cohort taken forthe legyons set agaynste fotemen ennemies metellus thus assembled company great parte oppressed woundes werynesse withdrew themselfe hyl named hyer place fayle suffre ennemies wont put trust flyght ouer come ferefull myndes remebre well ye disposed cowardly flee ye haue tentes city townes castels maner place defence wherto ye may ren refuge saue selfe contrary iugurth euery thing necessary expedient saue company men armes whiche wanted p last romayns wha vnderstode ther sure place wherto might fle also coude finde meanes fight enemy indifferently rutilius vnder captayne metellus xxxii chapter meane season bomylchar whome iugurth hadde made maister hys oliphantes parte hys foote menne haue wrytten assoone sawe rutilius whyche metellus sente vnto flodde muthull prouyde place theyre tentes ouerpassed hys companye lytle lytle conuayed ledde downe hys companye playne rutilius hasted hym towarde flodde commaunded metellus bomylchar set hys companye order araye styll quyetlye matter case requyred meane time forgatte searche espyes metellus dydde waye rutilius toke toward sayd flodde maner behaued hym selfe guided hys armye wherfore vnderstode epyes rutilius co pany take place said flod wher wold abide voide busines quiet douting peril syde vnderstode yt crye bataile betwene iugurth metellus encresed feared lest rutilius vnderstode therof wolde leue place flodde retourne batayle socour felowes ieopardy consideracion bomilchar ordered army nere togyder craft bycause mystrusted courage men boldnes great confidence therfore nowe agayne deuyded abrode muche larger proceded towarde tentes rutilius thintent lette hym company euery syde prepared towarde rescous metellus rutilyus company suspectynge peryll sodaynlie victorie coward rude vncrafty exalteth enioyeth may bost themself mennes dedes worthynesse cotrary wyse partie whiche ouercom though many good warryours noble worthy men yet ar reputed coward without
